This is a good, new spot for lighter Asian fare. I went for one of their special poke plates which had salmon, squid, octopus, tuna and yellowtail. The sauce was light and didn't overpower the fish.

The one issue was the timing of the meals coming out. They were busy but one of the six meals never came. Once we brought it up, they rectified it and gave coupons for our next visit. Overall it's a good spot for a change of pace up in the area.< /text>

<date>1571871915661< /date><rate>5<//rate>< Text>
This place is a family favorite. It's always been great and delicious.  We've tried a variety of dishes and they're all wonderful. Two things set this sushi restaurant apart from others:
1. You don't just have to rely on just soy sauce, they have delicious sauces that bring out the flavor of the rolls, without overwhelming it such as ponzu yuzu, eel sauce, spicy or sweet mayo, etc.
2. Their non-spicy sushi rolls are actually not spicy.  I've come across spicy items (wasabi or a dash of sriracha) mixed into non spicy rolls far too often at other sushi restaurants. Their regular spicy rolls are also not overwhelming.</Text>

< Text>
Don't be fooled by any good reviews this establishment has. If you actually take the time to read the reviews, you will notice that all the bad ones say stuff pertaining to the actual medical work....i.e. "they pulled the wrong tooth".....and all the good reviews pertain to how nice the staff was i.e. "Ingrid was very nice here's 5 stars"

The reason for this is that in order to raise their horrible rating,  they developed a strategy. The strategy begins at the dental office, where low status employees beg you for good reviews. When you go there, plan on being asked by like 5 people, from the receptionist all the way down to the janitor,  for a good review on google. They approach you with a card in hand, with their name written on it and say "will you please go to google and leave me a good review it really helps?" They do this throughout your appointment, but especially at the start, before you even have anything to base your rating on. They are pretty aggressive about it.

The reason for this behavior is this: if they get enough people to give them five stars because  "Maria was friendly", then hopefully it will drown out the seriously bad reviews,  like "the doctor was careless and rushed through my work, resulting in a new problem tooth that now requires extraction that wasnt neededn before "

This is the strategy that keeps their business afloat. If they didn't actively solicit good reviews for minor things, their whole review page would be full of patients sincerely unhappy with the medical work they received.

I commented about their bad work on a random Facebook group and within a day got 7 likes. Because people who know the truth know this place Is garbage.

If you must go.....absolutely don't let the young Indian or middle eastern girl doctors work on you. These girls have no business being in the dental field, let alone being doctors at all. Beware! Especially if you're poor, because if they think you can't afford  lawyer to get justice, they will  exploit this, and give you rushed,  second hand work.
Literally the worst medical establishment on the face of this earth. They're biggest concern isn't providing patients with good care, but rather rush them through and make the most profit with the cheapest,  fastest work.

This place sucks. And I hope I can save people the pain and suffering of learning the hard way. When it comes to teeth, you want to make sure you have a doctor who cares about their patients,  and these doctors don't fit that description in the least bit.< /Text>

This is my second review for Western Dental. It feels like my last review was treated with a level of dismisivness which i found irritating, and therefore gave me the desire to write a new review, addressing the issues I have.

First off, I should mention that I do not recommend this business to anyone who cares about receiving quality dental work. Honestly, if I could, I would have given this place a zero out of 5...but 1 is the lowest score I could give. I believe that medical doctors have a responsibility to provide their patients with the best care possible. Doctors get paid a pretty nice paycheck, and even on their worst day, I feel like its their obligation to provide the best quality work to ALL PATIENTS, despite the type of insurance they have, or the financial status of the patient etc.

The funny thing is, there are a million good dentists who provide great quality work. Unfortunately for me (and anyone else who chose this establishment), I picked the one in a million dentist that is actually no good!

Western Dental has responded to my original review, pretty much with a summary of all the good things I said, and several excuses as to why their subprime treatment is actually 100% my fault.

I dont have lawyer money to take Western Dental to court at the moment, but at least I can warn others of this place so they don't have to go through the same thing, and suffer due to a young doctor's neglect.

Ive already told my story herr but in a nutshell: I needed a bunch of extractions.....they specified which teeth needed extractions, and which were salvageable, by drilling and filling them.

They did the drilling/filling first.....and completed it on 2 separate dates. There are two young female doctors there, who I believe are of middle eastern descent.....i mention this because I dont know either of their names....they look like they could be sisters.

The first doctor girl did 3 drilling and fillings on the first appointment. The wait wasn't bad, thr doctor spent a good chunk of time making sure her work was done correctly, like a good doctor. I had no problems with any of her work, and left a happy patient.

The next time, I got 2 drilling and fillings from the other doctor. I do admit, it seems like they are overworked, which could lead to poor work, due to fatigue....but on the other hand, i work construction, and even after 8 physically demanding hours, i can still perform well.

So on this second day....i waited in the DENTIST CHAIR, not the waiting room,  for almost 2 hours. Finally, the second young doctor I previously described appeared, amd began aggressively drilling on my tooth. O was very surprised that these 3 teeth were completed in half the time it took the previous doctor to do 2 teeth. I wonder why that is? Is she just a better faster doctor? Haha, no.....she just didn't care to make sure she had done a good job....especially for a poor medi-cal recipient, who probably wont have the means to complain or sue if anything happens. What I should have done, and encourage anyone who still chooses to risk getting work for western dental, is video taped the procedure.....that way, an irresponsible doctor, or dental office will feel obligated to do a good job, since this would put them under scrutiny. Seriously guys.....your teeth are important....they cost an and a leg to completely replace.....and Western Dental WILL NOT try to make right with you any teeth they destroy....so keep the camera on with these guys.

Anyways.....the next couple days, both the latest fillings fell out. Upon doing a google search, I learned that this is VERY UNCOMMON, and probably due to poor dental work, which fit with my feeling of the work being super rushed.

Later on, the other young doctor girl tried to make excuses for her colleague, placing the blame all on me, but this was later.

Im out of characters....will write a part 2.</review>

I felt very uncomfortable and didnt want to talk about it right that second. I felt this was pretty obvious, but they were kind of insistent. That's ok, but here's what Dr. BS told me.

First she tried to say that they never drilled and filled those teeth, period. I guess she was hoping that I was someone with very low intelligence and bad short term memory...
But unfortunately for her, I dont have either of those qualities. Therefore I informed her of the fact that I remembered the procedure perfectly. She tried to argue with me about it a little more, then switched excuses, now saying they did do the fillings, but their strategy is to "try and fill them, not knowing of the cavity is too far gone for it to hold or not....and that if it falls out its just luck of the draw."......now im like wondering "what's going on here? Lol! Is this even a real doctor?"

What kind of doctor would say something, switch stories completely, and then provide false information about the procedure. And she became quiet when I told her that if they intended on extracting the tooth,the would have made the denture to include the tooth that now all the sudden had to be extracted.
What really happened is the first incompetent doctor saw i was a medi cal recipient and therefore rushed through my work. And when you do a bad job on drilling, the fillings fall out. And since she drilled so much out, now I lost a tooth that would cost 4 grand to replace.
I took my dentures and left. Im not letting these doctors who dont seem to know what they're doing or atleast dont care touch my teeth ever again.

< text>
This place by far the best place, it has a nice set up. The food I order was really good as I expected. The noodle broth was well balance and has that nice soothing flavor, that's the first thing I do before I eat it. Is to taste the broth first to see how the flavor is before I eat the noodle. 1). As you walk in how is the atmosphere and set up like.
2).Greeting and service.
3).The menu was nicely done.
4). Ordering was properly taken care of.
5). The food was really good and flavorful.
